alſo myne owne doe poſſeſſe worlde wylbe duringe lyfe thy truſtie ſeruante otherwyſe doe aſſure thee may doe anye perſwaſion thou mayeſt vſe chiefely turckes alwayes enemyes y• chriſtianes euel neighbour alſo wherfore wyl put hazarde god hath gyuen maruell ryghte thyne poſſeſſe dothe appertaine chriſtians althoughe dyd apertaine father myne chriſtian haue lawfully recouered wt ſworde hand alſo ſhoulde prouoke thee becomme chriſtian poſſeſſion townes gouernement dothe apertaine chriſtianes infydelles wherfore againe beſeche thee thou wylte becomme chriſtian otherwyſe wyll contynually drino whoſe death scanderbeg ſory y• ben alwaye gréate fryndſhippe betwene dyed withoute child scanderbeg determyned ſuccede hym ſtate ye deceaſe ladie boſſa mother vertue certaine couenantes ye betwene notwithſtanding ladie boſſa meane lieutenante scutari agreed senate veniſe vpō certaine condition delyuered ye dagnio reſt ſtate scanderbeg greatly offendyd aſſembled al hys power went perſon beſeged dagnio lefte withſtanding vpō confines truſtie frind countye vurana one captaines garde therof wt thre thouſand ſouldiours lieutenante scutarie vnderſtoode aduertized senate therof receaued commiſſion leuie armie wher vpon toke oute scutarie many bandes italian leuied great number albaneſes made general armie worthie damel sebenico ſone al thinges redie marched towarde scanderbeg ſone herde hereof paſſed ryuer drino al armie goe towarde venetian armie encoūtre ſpake ſouldiours maner folowethscan ſouldiours compainons armes ſo man maye lawfully demaunde righte withoute wronge anye man truely haue demaunded righte beſeged dagnio taken ſtraicte valley therof doe beliue haue done iniurie al senate veniſe rather wronged notwtſtanding haue partely excuſed conſideringe falſe information hath ben made vnto abſence contrarie partie truely perſwade ſelfe iuſt moſt chriſtian knowing great affection good wyl ye haue alwaye borne wolde neuer haue concluded preiudice yf firſt vnderſtode right notwithſtanding haue nowe addreſſyd armie againſt muſt nedes daye fighte againſt chriſtians dede greatly againſt wyl wherfore nowe ſay vnto behoueth fighte circumſpectly valiantly haue done anye tyme el conſydering haue doe men doe farre excede turcks valewe yet hope god victorie ſhalbe wherfore doe commaūde ſhal haue broken man ſley anye take priſoners folowe chaſe euen gate scutari thus ſayd ſpake highethe bettayle betwene scan venetianes ſainge folowe marched armie battayle ioyned venetianes fighte betwene contynued wt great obſtinatie ende scanderbeg diſordered put flighte folowing chaſe euen gate scutari dyd ſley none chaſe toke great number priſoners eſpecially men acompte al preſented scāderbeg lyke noble prince cauſed al wel entertained ſent home wit houte ranſom al thoſe priſoners cauſed detēyne two men acompte one simone vulcatal countrey • cutari andre humoi brother ye captaine croia ſent owne countrey kepte priſoners forte ye great ſtrength called pietra bianca cōmaunded wel vſed great prouiſion appointed vnto scanderbeg paſſed armye throughe al countre appertained venetianes thinckinge haue taken coulde whervpō fortified raſed citie name balezzo ben diſtroied attilla flagello di dio fortified walles trench baſtiōnes furniſhed al kinde menition valiante men appointed captaine one hys captaynes named marino spā man muche worthynes ye ende ſhoulde contynual courſes ſpoyleiudgemēt scanderbeg impoueriſhe countre kepe continual doubte eſtabliſhed order retorned ye ſeege dagnio scutari vnderſtanding ye marino span gone forthe balezzo went thyther al ſpede ſpoyled citie foundation wherwith scanderbeg beinge greatly offendyd deſtroied al countrey scutari turcke venderſtode scanderbeg warres venetianes conſydering countre laie betwene two mighty enemy excedinly glad thinckinge venetianes great force wolde ſone chaſe scanderbeg oute countrey wherefore ſent commaundement muſtaffa laye vpon cōfines xv horſemen goe ſpoyle al scāderbegs countre yet al muſtaffa canſydering bandes scāderbeg lying vpon frontier redynes wolde goe furder place called dronich ſet vp tentes lying armie encamped helde countrey contynual feare wherof ſone scanderbeg aduertizement departed dagnio two thouſand ſouldiours went thre thouſand ſouldiours laye vpō confines whē exhorted behaue themſelues valiantly put order aſſailed ye turckes obedience yet notwithſtanding city defended ſelues chiefely driuazzo whyles amesabeg nephewe scanderbeg ſpoiled countre drinazzo worthy andre ſurnamed angelo deſcended romanes whiche tyme paſſed onles driuaſto excuſe preſent rencoūtre ende scanderbeg made peace venetianes vpō condition ſhoulde reſtore vnto al thoſe place taken recompence therof ſhoulde haue one part valey ſtraſcte scutari veniſe ſorte foloweth right honorable lorde ambaſſadours opinion ſuche wyſe man louethe dede muſt nedes loue alwaie peraduenture prouerbe hathe herof begynninge whiche ſaythe diſcorde frinds vnderſtande make leſſe acompte mine owne cō modities thers doe make preſēt al ye mine haue difference doe holde ſelfe wel cōtented contynually poſſeſſion furder wyl feare turcke truſte god defende preſentes token goodwyl bare senate veniſe ſame tyme scanderbeg made great courſe turckes countrey burned ſpoyled al ye countre paſſed thorowe brought great proie thence whervpon turcke called vnto hande scanderbeg mortal enemie wherfore doe nowe determyne reuenged employe al force poſſyble againſt ſo muche coulde neuer gyue ouerthrowe hathe alwayes triumphed ouer people ouer venetianes alſo one redie woe ſhal redie muſtres scanderbeg ſpedyly aduiſed great preparatiō al ſpede furniſhed citie al kynde neceſſaries good ſouldiours albaneſes great experience faith gaue general vurana aforeſaid gone zachuria groppa one countes ſouldiours declared vnto ye coūtie euen came paſſe wherfore counte hys armye departed ſpede went enrampe place farre scāderbeg retorned nexte morninge toke kinge companie myngled ſouldiours auoyde ſtrife went folowinge tracte enemie ſhorte tyme diſcouered cauſed marche one ſyde frederick duke vrbine lieutenante pope armie alexandre sforza lieutenante brother duke milane deſyred erneſtly y• mought ſo paſſe ouer whē al thing order marched citie called troia duke iohn countie iames armye citie called nucera troia viii myles acordinge meſure apulia betwene whiche two city moūtaine called segiano frō troia two myles nucera viii myles scanderbeg therfore knowinge ye army muſt fighte betwene thoſe two city roſe vp nighte wt ſouldiours went toke hill furniſhed wt men ſufficient defende ende yf peraduenture king power ſhoulde ouerthrowen mought take hill defend ſelues coūtie iames dede ſkylfull greate experience warres ment alſo take ſame hyll therfore departed alſo morninge betyme take hill founde scanderbeg alredye taken ſorie ſayde certaine moſt truſtie frinds oute al hope victorie notwithſtandinge lefte dyd euery reſpecte office duetie good captaine exhortinge encoraginge ſouldiours puttinge alſo order acordinge tyme place nexte morning determyned gyue battayle made redie bothe ſydes enbattayled peoplethe batbetwene duke iohn scan encountred fyghte betwene moſt terrible contynued tyll euening ye ende duke armie ſo ouerthrowen ſpoiled glad moughte retorne fraunce wt ſhame diſhonor loſſe maner frenſhe bandes lykewyſe countie iames wt infortunate noble men apuglia fled thorowe moſt difficulte paſſages euery man waye greate grace god y• eſcaped lyues kynge deliuered enemy great glorie triumphe throughe worthynes magnanime puiſſante victoriouſe prince scanderbeg aforeſayde king ferrante rode wt scanderbeg ſee yf coulde recouer city townes loſte entred naples great triumphe afterwarde wente iorney notwithſtanding manye city townes continued former purpoſe wolde wiſe obey king ferrante ſayde wolde rather dye weapones handes yelde wycked handes wel aſſured wolde reuenged wolde obſerue promiſe contented yelde scanderbeg vpon faithefull promes ende kyng scanderbeg talked togyther agreed kyng ſhoulde ſwere performe promes ſhoulde made name scanderbeg ſhoulde promes ſubiectes aſſure therof otherwyſe wolde yelde wolde fyghte oute vttermoſt ſemed vnto thinge moſt vnſemely chriſtian prince breake faythe ſeale ſaluation euery chriſtian bounde obſerue euen enemyes kyng ſwore openly wolde performe euery reſpecte ſo euer hys good father scanthe othe kinge ferrante ſhoulde promiſe done scanderbeg wente aſſured kyng ſhoulde performe promes euery reſpecte ſhoulde vſe fryndes louinge ſubiectes meanes wherof al place wherſoeuer came yelded vnto ſone scanderbeg entred place cauſed ſet vp enſeignes kinge ferrante made ſwere fidelitie obedience ye king meane tyme fuſano sicillian man great prowes toke fuſano alſo wolde ſet libertie mought haue meanes eſcape commaunded nephewe yelde forte handes scanderbeg done scanderbeg ſet fuſano libertie ſuffred ronne waye scanderbeg recouered againe kynges cuſtume gyue meate drincke ſubiectes came aboute anye ſutes thither entertayned honorably ſuche came viſyte chiefe coūcellers ſate alwaies owne table euery man degree often tymes wolde cauſe drincke confynes viſite captaine lefte whē went apuglia made great banckettes captaine ſouldiours gaue diuerſe fryndes thiefe ſouldiours great gyftes ſome gaue apparell clothe golde others ſylke ſome ſcarlate colour ſome gaue horſes others money ſome one thinge others acordinge euery mannes deſeruinges ſo euery man well pleaſed beſyde neuer denyed almes anye pore man aſked chriſtes ſake thoſe dayes gaue great almes chiefely ſonnes thoſe noble men byn chaſed oute countres turckes dyuerſe noble ſtraungers came farre gaue onely money apparell alſo poſſeſſiones maintaine honeſtly lyue lyke faithfull touching thy highnes ſaieth yu wylte henceforth call prince epirotts ſhal offend thou ſhalte doe right giue tytle god goodnes hathe gyuen owne honor thy highnes requireth onely ſonne iohn ſolaſe mother thinge alſo maye graunte hauinge noyſſue onelye carefull otherwiſe aūſwere thee thy maieſrie ſaieth thou deſyreſt ſeme perſonally ye great frindſhippe hath ben betwyne v longe tyme ſay magnificent scanderbeg prince epirotts haue none occaſion ſende thee greting wyſhe helthe well thou haſt broken peace made betwyne v alſo thou haſt holden thy promiſed faythe haſt done ſo manye thee vpon fayth wyll obſerue promes euery condition neuer moleſt thee alwaies profytable frindely thee redie honor otherwiſe doe aſſure thee wyll leue enterpriſe wyll contynually folowe plague thee ſuche ſorte yf thou eſcape thy lyfe wyl baniſhe thy countrey ſhal ſeen whyther venetianes able maintaine ye againſt thou beinge ſymple meane prince parte albania whiche thou nowe poſeſſiſt emperour kynge prince ſo manye power countreys thou ſhalte neuer able wtſtand furye wherfore haue regarde thy ſelfe make peace good ende thou mayeſt dye lorde thy countrey leaue honor thy poſteritie otherwyſe ſhalbe thy hindrance thou maiſt gyue credite ſeruante abaſſadour muſtaffa thinges ſhall ſaye vnto thee conſtantinople 7 maye 1463 scanderbeg herde ambaſſadour red letter turcke ſent wrote aunſwere
